incremental push.\n// Pilot uses multiple registries - for example each K8S cluster is a registry\n// instance. Each registry is responsible for tracking a set\n// of endpoints associated with mesh services, and calling the EDSUpdate on changes.\n// A registry may group endpoints for a service in smaller subsets - for example by\n// deployment, or to deal with very large number of endpoints for a service. We want\n// to avoid passing around large objects - like full list of endpoints for a registry,\n// or the full list of endpoints for a service across registries, since it limits\n// scalability.\n//\n// Future optimizations will include grouping the endpoints by labels, gateway or region to\n// reduce the time when subsetting or split-horizon is used. This design assumes pilot\n// tracks all endpoints in the mesh and they fit in RAM - so limit is few M endpoints.\n// It is possible to split the endpoint tracking in future.\ntype XDSUpdater interface {\n\t// EDSUpdate is called when the list of endpoints or labels in a Service is changed.\n\t// For each cluster and hostname, the full list of active endpoints (including empty list)\n\t// must be sent. The shard name is used as a key - current implementation is using the\n\t// registry name.\n\tEDSUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, entry []*IstioEndpoint)\n\n\t// EDSCacheUpdate is called when the list of endpoints or labels in a Service is changed.\n\t// For each cluster and hostname, the full list of active endpoints (including empty list)\n\t// must be sent. The shard name is used as a key - current implementation is using the\n\t// registry name.\n\t// Note: the difference with `EDSUpdate` is that it only update the cache rather than requesting a push\n\tEDSCacheUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, entry []*IstioEndpoint)\n\n\t// SvcUpdate is called when a service definition is updated/deleted.\n\tSvcUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, event Event)\n\n\t// ConfigUpdate is called to notify the XDS server of config updates and request a push.\n\t// The requests may be collapsed and throttled.\n\tConfigUpdate(req *PushRequest)\n\n\t// ProxyUpdate is called to notify the XDS server to send a push to the specified proxy.\n\t// The requests may be collapsed and throttled.\n\tProxyUpdate(clusterID cluster.ID, ip string)\n\n\t// RemoveShard removes all endpoints for the given shard key\n\tRemoveShard(shardKey ShardKey)\n}\n\n// PushRequest defines a request to push to proxies\n// It is used to send updates to the config update debouncer and pass to the PushQueue.\ntype PushRequest struct {\n\t// Full determines whether a full push is required or not. If false, an incremental update will be sent.\n\t// Incremental pushes:\n\t// * Do not recompute the push context\n\t// * Do not recompute proxy state (such as ServiceInstances)\n\t// * Are not reported in standard metrics such as push time\n\t// As a result, configuration updates should never be incremental. Generally, only EDS will set this, but\n\t// in the future SDS will as well.\n\tFull bool\n\n\t// ConfigsUpdated keeps track of configs that have changed.\n\t// This is used as an optimization to avoid unnecessary pushes to proxies that are scoped with a Sidecar.\n\t// If this is empty, then all proxies will get an update.\n\t// Otherwise only proxies depend on these configs will get an update.\n\t// The kind of resources are defined in pkg/config/schemas.\n\tConfigsUpdated sets.Set[ConfigKey]\n\n\tAddressesUpdated sets.Set[string]\n\n\t// Push stores the push context to use for the update. This may initially be nil, as we will\n\t// debounce changes before a PushContext is eventually created.\n\tPush *PushContext\n\n\t// Start represents the time a push was started. This represents the time of adding to the PushQueue.\n\t// Note that this does not include time spent debouncing.\n\tStart time.Time\n\n\t// Reason represents the reason for requesting a push. This should only be a fixed set of values,\n\t// to avoid unbounded cardinality in metrics. If this is not set, it may be automatically filled in later.\n\t// There should only be multiple reasons if the push request is the result of two distinct triggers, rather than\n\t// classifying a single trigger as having multiple reasons.\n\tReason ReasonStats\n\n\t// Delta defines the resources that were added or removed as part of this push request.\n\t// This is set only on requests from the client which change the set of resources they (un)subscribe from.\n\tDelta ResourceDelta\n\n\t// Forced defines that configs should be generated and pushed regardless if they have changed or not.\n\tForced bool\n}\n\ntype ResourceDelta = xds.ResourceDelta\n\ntype ReasonStats map[TriggerReason]int\n\nfunc NewReasonStats(reasons ...TriggerReason) ReasonStats {\n\tret := make(ReasonStats)\n\tfor _, reason := range reasons {\n\t\tret.Add(reason)\n\t}\n\treturn ret\n}\n\nfunc (r ReasonStats) Add(reason TriggerReason) {\n\tr[reason]++\n}\n\nfunc (r ReasonStats) Merge(other ReasonStats) {\n\tfor reason, count := range other {\n\t\tr[reason] += count\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (r ReasonStats) CopyMerge(other ReasonStats) ReasonStats {\n\tif len(r) == 0 {\n\t\treturn other\n\t}\n\tif len(other) == 0 {\n\t\treturn r\n\t}\n\n\tmerged := make(ReasonStats, len(r)+len(other))\n\tmerged.Merge(r)\n\tmerged.Merge(other)\n\n\treturn merged\n}\n\nfunc (r ReasonStats) Count() int {\n\tvar ret int\n\tfor _, count := range r {\n\t\tret += count\n\t}\n\treturn ret\n}\n\nfunc (r ReasonStats) Has(reason TriggerReason) bool {\n\treturn r[reason] > 0\n}\n\ntype TriggerReason string\n","numLines":250,"startLine":200,"totalLines":2642}}}

true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif servicesChanged {\n\t\t// Services have changed. initialize service registry\n\t\tps.initServiceRegistry(env, pushReq.ConfigsUpdated)\n\t} else {\n\t\t// make sure we copy oldPushContext.GatewayAPIController\n\t}\n\n\tif virtualServicesChanged {\n\t\tps.initVirtualServices(env)\n\t} else {\n\t\tps.virtualServiceIndex = oldPushContext.virtualServiceIndex\n\t}\n\n\tif {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01GLqGoKviLvYiDegoH6Bjkk","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01NARA8AqA4afNtj5Q9e6rQ8","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Istio Pilot Discovery Service Architecture\n\n## Overview\n\nThe Istio Pilot Discovery Service is the control plane component responsible for serving dynamic configuration to data plane proxies (Envoy sidecars and gateways) through xDS (Envoy Discovery Service) APIs. Pilot translates high-level Istio networking resources (VirtualServices, DestinationRules, Sidecars, etc.) into Envoy-specific configurations (Clusters, Routes, Listeners, Endpoints) and maintains a fleet-wide view of services across multiple Kubernetes clusters.\n\nThis document explains the architecture of four core subsystems:\n\n1. **DiscoveryServer** — Pilot's gRPC server implementing Envoy's xDS protocol\n2. **ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service)** — The bidirectional stream handler managing individual proxy connections\n3. **PushContext** — The immutable configuration snapshot used during a push cycle\n4. **Service Registry** — The service discovery layer integrating Kubernetes and multi-cluster data\n\n---\n\n## 1. DiscoveryServer — The xDS gRPC Server\n\n### Overview\n\nThe `DiscoveryServer` is Pilot's core gRPC server that implements Envoy's xDS v3 protocol. It serves as the central hub for pushing configuration changes to all connected proxies, managing client connections, and coordinating the push pipeline.\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`\n\n### Key Responsibilities\n\n- **gRPC Protocol Implementation:** Registers as an `AggregatedDiscoveryServiceServer` (v3) and handles bidirectional xDS streams\n- **Client Connection Management:** Tracks active proxy connections in `adsClients` map (keyed by connection ID)\n- **Push Coordination:** Debounces configuration changes, enforces rate limits, and serializes concurrent pushes\n- **Cache Management:** Maintains an `XdsCache` for generated xDS resources to avoid recomputation\n- **Readiness Enforcement:** Ensures all caches are synced before accepting client connections\n\n### Initialization\n\n```go\n// Created with environment and cluster aliases\nds := NewDiscoveryServer(env *model.Environment, clusterAliases map[string]string, debugger *krt.DebugHandler)\n```\n\nThe `DiscoveryServer` initializes with:\n- `Env`: The Istio environment containing service registry, config store, and push context\n- `Generators`: Map of custom `XdsResourceGenerator` implementations (extensible per resource type or per client)\n- `ProxyNeedsPush`: Optional filter function to skip pushes for specific proxies\n- `concurrentPushLimit`: Semaphore limiting concurrent push operations (controlled by `PILOT_PUSH_THROTTLE`)\n- `RequestRateLimit`: Rate limiter preventing thundering herd of incoming requests\n- `DebounceOptions`: Configuration for debouncing and merging rapid updates\n- `Cache`: XDS resource cache (optional, controlled by `PILOT_ENABLE_XDS_CACHE`)\n\n### The Push Pipeline\n\nWhen Istio configuration changes, the push follows this pipeline:\n\n```\nConfig Change Event\n    ↓\nConfigUpdate() [non-blocking, enqueued to pushChannel]\n    ↓\nhandleUpdates() goroutine [debouncing + merging]\n    ↓\nPush() [full or incremental]\n    ├─→ initPushContext() [rebuild config snapshot if full push]\n    ├─→ dropCacheForRequest() [clear affected cache entries]\n    ├─→ AdsPushAll() [enqueue to pushQueue for all proxies]\n    ↓\nsendPushes() goroutine [process pushQueue with concurrency limits]\n    ├─→ PushCh() [send Event to each connection's push channel]\n    ↓\nConnection.Push() [serialize per-connection push logic]\n```\n\n### Debouncing and Rate Control\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` - `debounce()` function\n\nThe discovery server implements two layers of debouncing:\n\n1. **Event Debouncing** (`handleUpdates`)\n   - Groups rapid configuration events within `DebounceAfter` window (default 100ms)\n   - Merges multiple events into a single `PushRequest`\n   - Enforces maximum delay of `debounceMax` (default 10s) to prevent indefinite delays\n   - Special handling for EDS (Endpoint Discovery Service) updates, which can bypass debouncing if `enableEDSDebounce` is false\n\n2. **Push Concurrency Control**\n   - `concurrentPushLimit` semaphore restricts simultaneous xDS push operations (default: 100)\n   - Prevents overwhelming the system with too many concurrent computations\n   - `RequestRateLimit` (rate limiter) throttles incoming xDS requests per second\n\n### Cache Management\n\nThe `Cache` field holds the XDS resource cache, implemented as:\n- `TypedXdsCache`: Maps (proxy metadata, resource type) → generated resource\n- Cleared selectively on config changes via `dropCacheForRequest()`\n- Fully cleared on forced/unknown updates\n- Accessed during resource generation to avoid recomputation\n\n### Metrics and Monitoring\n\nThe DiscoveryServer tracks:\n- `InboundUpdates`: Total config updates received\n- `CommittedUpdates`: Updates incorporated into the push context (subset of inbound)\n- Push times, debounce delays, queue depths\n- Per-proxy push status and errors (stored in `PushContext.ProxyStatus`)\n- Periodic metrics refresh every 10 seconds\n\n### Lifecycle\n\n```go\n// Startup\nserver.Start(stopCh <-chan struct{})\n    ├─→ WorkloadEntryController.Run()    // handle auto-registered workloads\n    ├─→ handleUpdates()                   // debounce config changes\n    ├─→ periodicRefreshMetrics()          // refresh push metrics\n    ├─→ sendPushes()                      // process push queue\n    └─→ Cache.Run()                       // background cache cleanup\n\n// Readiness\nserver.CachesSynced()  // called when all config stores are synced\nserver.IsServerReady() // checked before accepting connections\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. ADS and the Connection Model\n\n### Overview\n\nThe Aggregated Discovery Service (ADS) is Pilot's implementation of Envoy's bidirectional streaming gRPC protocol. Each connected proxy maintains a persistent stream with Pilot, and ADS coordinates what configuration gets pushed to each proxy individually.\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`\n\n### The Connection Type\n\n```go\ntype Connection struct {\n    xds.Connection\n    node       *core.Node                    // Original Envoy node metadata\n    proxy      *model.Proxy                  // Parsed proxy metadata\n    deltaStream DeltaDiscoveryStream         // For delta/incremental mode\n    stream     DiscoveryStream                // For state-of-world mode\n    s          *DiscoveryServer\n    ids        []string                      // Auth identities\n}\n```\n\nThe `Connection` wraps the gRPC stream with:\n- **Proxy Metadata:** The `Proxy` object contains workload labels, locality, service targets, sidecar scope\n- **Stream Type:** Either `stream` (state-of-the-world) or `deltaStream` (incremental delta mode)\n- **Request Channel:** Buffered channel for push events from DiscoveryServer\n\n### Connection Lifecycle\n\n#### 1. Stream Establishment (`Stream()`)\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) Stream(stream xds.DiscoveryStream) error {\n    // Check server readiness\n    if !s.IsServerReady() {\n        return Unavailable error\n    }\n\n    // Rate limit enforcement\n    if err := s.WaitForRequestLimit(...); err != nil {\n        return ResourceExhausted error\n    }\n\n    // Authentication\n    ids, err := s.authenticate(stream.Context())\n\n    // Initialize push context if needed\n    s.globalPushContext().InitContext(...)\n\n    // Create connection wrapper\n    conn := newConnection(peerAddr, stream)\n    conn.s = s\n    conn.ids = ids\n\n    // Delegate to xds.Stream (handles stream I/O loop)\n    return xds.Stream(conn)\n}\n```\n\nThe stream handling is delegated to the `xds.Stream()` function from the `go-control-plane` library, which manages the gRPC stream's read/write loops while calling into our `Connection` methods for protocol handling.\n\n#### 2. Connection Initialization (`initConnection()`)\n\nWhen the first discovery request arrives (containing node metadata), Pilot initializes the proxy:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) initConnection(node *core.Node, con *Connection, identities []string) error {\n    // Parse node metadata and create Proxy object\n    proxy, err := s.initProxyMetadata(node)\n\n    // Apply cluster aliases (for multi-cluster scenarios)\n    if alias, exists := s.ClusterAliases[proxy.Metadata.ClusterID]; exists {\n        proxy.Metadata.ClusterID = alias\n    }\n\n    // Capture current push context as baseline for this proxy\n    proxy.LastPushContext = s.globalPushContext()\n\n    // Assign connection ID\n    con.SetID(connectionID(proxy.ID))\n\n    // Authorize proxy\n    if err := s.authorize(con, identities); err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n\n    // Register connection (enables push targeting)\n    s.addCon(con.ID(), con)\n    defer con.MarkInitialized()\n\n    // Full initialization: compute sidecar scope, service targets, security policies\n    return s.initializeProxy(con)\n}\n```\n\n**Key Steps:**\n- **Metadata Parsing:** Extract cluster, namespace, workload labels from node metadata\n- **Cluster Alias Resolution:** Support for multi-cluster alias names\n- **Baseline PushContext:** Capture the current push context to ensure this proxy doesn't receive older pushes\n- **Registration:** Add to `adsClients` map to enable future push targeting\n- **Proxy Initialization:** Expensive computation like sidecar scope lookup happens here\n\n#### 3. Connection Shutdown (`closeConnection()`)\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) closeConnection(con *Connection) {\n    s.removeCon(con.ID())\n    s.WorkloadEntryController.OnDisconnect(con)\n}\n```\n\nRemoves the connection from the tracking map and notifies the workload entry controller (for auto-registration cleanup).\n\n### Request Processing\n\n#### `processRequest(req *DiscoveryRequest, con *Connection)`\n\nWhen a proxy sends a discovery request, Pilot determines which resources to send back:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) processRequest(req *DiscoveryRequest, con *Connection) error {\n    stype := v3.GetShortType(req.TypeUrl)  // e.g., \"CDS\" from cluster type URL\n\n    // Debug endpoints bypass normal processing\n    if strings.HasPrefix(req.TypeUrl, v3.DebugType) {\n        return s.pushXds(con, req.TypeUrl, ...)\n    }\n\n    // Update tracked watched resources\n    con.UpdateWatchedResource(req)\n\n    // Determine if proxy needs this push\n    if needsPush := computeNeedsPush(req, con); !needsPush {\n        return nil  // Skip if already satisfied\n    }\n\n    // Fetch or generate resources\n    return s.pushXds(con, req.TypeUrl, ...)\n}\n```\n\n**Resource Type Handling:** Pilot handles multiple xDS resource types:\n- **CDS (Cluster Discovery Service):** Envoy cluster configurations (load balancing, circuit breakers)\n- **RDS (Route Discovery Service):** HTTP route configurations\n- **LDS (Listener Discovery Service):** Envoy listeners (inbound/outbound)\n- **EDS (Endpoint Discovery Service):** Service endpoint instances\n\n#### Push to Connection (`pushConnection()`)\n\nWhen a push is triggered, all relevant proxies receive updates via `pushConnection()`:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) pushConnection(con *Connection, ev *Event) error {\n    pushReq := ev.pushRequest\n\n    // Early filter: skip if proxy doesn't need this push\n    if filteredReq, ok := s.ProxyNeedsPush(con.proxy, pushReq); !ok {\n        return nil\n    }\n\n    // For each watched resource type\n    for typeUrl, watchedRes := range con.proxy.WatchedResources {\n        // Generate or fetch resources\n        res, logDetails, err := s.generateResources(con.proxy, typeUrl, filteredReq)\n\n        // Send response\n        response := &DiscoveryResponse{\n            TypeUrl:     typeUrl,\n            Resources:   res,\n            VersionInfo: generateVersionString(),\n            Nonce:       nonce(\"push\"),\n        }\n        con.Send(response)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### StartPush and Fleet-Wide Updates\n\nThe `AdsPushAll()` method initiates a fleet-wide push:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) AdsPushAll(req *model.PushRequest) {\n    s.adsClientsMutex.RLock()\n    for id, conn := range s.adsClients {\n        // Enqueue push for each proxy\n        s.pushQueue.Enqueue(conn, req)\n    }\n    s.adsClientsMutex.RUnlock()\n}\n```\n\nThis is non-blocking; the actual serialization happens in `sendPushes()` goroutine, which reads from `pushQueue` and respects the `concurrentPushLimit`.\n\n---\n\n## 3. PushContext — Configuration Snapshot and Translation\n\n### Overview\n\n`PushContext` is an immutable snapshot of all Istio configuration, services, and security policies at a point in time. It's computed once per push cycle and shared across all proxy generations to ensure consistency.\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`\n\n### What PushContext Holds\n\n```go\ntype PushContext struct {\n    // Service information\n    ServiceIndex serviceIndex          // Services indexed by namespace, host, and visibility\n    serviceAccounts map[key][]string   // Service account mappings\n\n    // Routing configuration\n    virtualServiceIndex virtualServiceIndex    // Virtual services indexed by gateway/namespace\n    destinationRuleIndex destinationRuleIndex  // Destination rules (traffic policies)\n\n    // Ingress and gateway configuration\n    gatewayIndex gatewayIndex         // Kubernetes gateways and Istio gateways\n\n    // Policy and extension configuration\n    AuthnPolicies *AuthenticationPolicies      // RequestAuthentication, PeerAuthentication\n    AuthzPolicies *AuthorizationPolicies       // AuthorizationPolicy rules\n    envoyFiltersByNamespace map[string][]*EnvoyFilterWrapper\n    wasmPluginsByNamespace map[string][]*WasmPluginWrapper\n    Telemetry *Telemetries            // Telemetry (traces, metrics, logs)\n    ProxyConfigs *ProxyConfigs         // ProxyConfig resources\n\n    // Network configuration\n    Mesh *meshconfig.MeshConfig        // Global mesh settings\n    Networks *meshconfig.MeshNetworks  // Multi-cluster network definitions\n    networkMgr *NetworkManager         // Gateway addresses per network\n\n    // Sidecar scoping\n    sidecarIndex sidecarIndex          // Workload-specific sidecar rules\n\n    // Metrics and status\n    ProxyStatus map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus\n    PushVersion string                 // Version identifier for this push\n\n    // Ambient support\n    ambientIndex AmbientIndexes        // Ambient mesh specific indexes\n\n    // Caching and resolution\n    JwtKeyResolver *JwksResolver       // JWKS public key resolver\n    GatewayAPIController GatewayController  // Gateway API resources\n}\n```\n\n### InitContext — Building the Snapshot\n\nWhen a full push is triggered, `initPushContext()` builds a new `PushContext`:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) initPushContext(req *model.PushRequest, oldPushContext *model.PushContext, version string) *model.PushContext {\n    push := model.NewPushContext()\n    push.PushVersion = version\n\n    // InitContext does the actual work\n    push.InitContext(s.Env, oldPushContext, req)\n    return push\n}\n```\n\nThe `InitContext()` method executes initialization in two paths:\n\n#### Full Context Creation\n\nIf no previous context exists or the update is forced:\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) createNewContext(env *Environment) {\n    ps.initServiceRegistry(env, nil)      // Load all services\n    ps.initKubernetesGateways(env)        // Load K8s Gateway API resources\n    ps.initVirtualServices(env)            // Index virtual services\n    ps.initDestinationRules(env)           // Index destination rules and traffic policies\n    ps.initAuthnPolicies(env)              // Load authentication policies\n    ps.initAuthorizationPolicies(env)      // Load authorization policies\n    ps.initTelemetry(env)                  // Load telemetry configurations\n    ps.initProxyConfigs(env)               // Load proxy configurations\n    ps.initWasmPlugins(env)                // Load WASM plugins\n    ps.initEnvoyFilters(env, nil, nil)     // Load Envoy filter patches\n    ps.initGateways(env)                   // Index gateways\n    ps.initAmbient(env)                    // Initialize ambient mesh indexes\n    ps.initSidecarScopes(env)              // Compute workload sidecar scopes (must be last)\n}\n```\n\n#### Incremental Context Update\n\nFor faster incremental updates, only changed configuration is recomputed:\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) updateContext(env *Environment, oldPushContext *model.PushContext, pushReq *model.PushRequest) {\n    // Analyze what changed\n    for conf := range pushReq.ConfigsUpdated {\n        switch conf.Kind {\n        case kind.ServiceEntry, kind.DNSName:\n            servicesChanged = true\n        case kind.VirtualService:\n            virtualServicesChanged = true\n        case kind.DestinationRule:\n            destinationRulesChanged = true\n        // ... other config types\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Recompute only affected parts\n    if servicesChanged {\n        ps.initServiceRegistry(env, pushReq.ConfigsUpdated)\n    } else {\n        ps.ServiceIndex = oldPushContext.ServiceIndex\n    }\n\n    if virtualServicesChanged {\n        ps.initVirtualServices(env)\n    } else {\n        ps.virtualServiceIndex = oldPushContext.virtualServiceIndex\n    }\n    // ... similar for other resources\n\n    // Sidecar scopes may need recomputation if services/routing changed\n    if servicesChanged || virtualServicesChanged || destinationRulesChanged || sidecarsChanged {\n        ps.initSidecarScopes(env)\n    } else {\n        ps.sidecarIndex = oldPushContext.sidecarIndex\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThis optimization is crucial for scalability — most pushes are incremental EDS updates that don't require rebuilding the entire routing configuration.\n\n### Configuration Translation: Istio → Envoy\n\nThe `PushContext` is then used by resource generators to translate Istio resources into Envoy configurations. The translation happens in two stages:\n\n#### 1. Service Registry to EDS\n\nWhen services or endpoints change, the registry triggers EDS (Endpoint Discovery Service) updates:\n\n```\nK8s Service/Pod Change\n    ↓\nServiceRegistry.WorkItem() [watches K8s resources]\n    ↓\nXDSUpdater.EDSUpdate() [or SvcUpdate()]\n    ↓\nConfigUpdate(PushRequest{Full: false}) [incremental EDS push]\n    ↓\nEDS Generator generates() [endpoints from ServiceIndex]\n```\n\n#### 2. VirtualService + DestinationRule to CDS/RDS\n\nPilot translates Istio's routing policies into Envoy clusters and routes:\n\n- **VirtualService** → Envoy **RouteConfiguration** (RDS)\n  - Routes matching on HTTP host/path to destination clusters\n  - Retries, timeouts, traffic shifting\n\n- **DestinationRule** → Envoy **Cluster** modifications (CDS)\n  - Load balancer policy, outlier detection\n  - TLS settings, connection pooling\n\n- **VirtualService** + **DestinationRule** + **DestinationRule subsets** → Multiple **Clusters** per destination\n\n**Source Code:**\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/cluster.go` — Cluster (CDS) generation\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/route/route.go` — Route (RDS) generation\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/cluster_builder.go` — Cluster building from Istio resources\n\n#### 3. Sidecar Scope Filtering\n\nFor each proxy, the `SidecarScope` (from the Sidecar resource) determines:\n- Which services are reachable from this workload\n- Which inbound/outbound listeners to create\n- Which traffic policies apply\n\n```go\n// Computed during InitContext\nsidecarScope := ps.GetSidecarScope(proxy)\n\n// Used during resource generation\nif !sidecarScope.IsVisible(service) {\n    return  // Skip this service in CDS/RDS for this proxy\n}\n```\n\n### Extension Points in PushContext\n\n1. **Custom Generators:** The `Generators` map in `DiscoveryServer` can override resource generation per proxy type or resource type\n2. **ProxyNeedsPush Filter:** Custom logic to skip pushes for certain proxies\n3. **Telemetry Plugins:** Extensions in `Telemetry` configuration\n4. **WASM Plugins:** Extensions specified in `WasmPlugin` resources\n5. **EnvoyFilter Patches:** Customize generated Envoy configuration via patches\n\n### Metrics and Error Tracking\n\nPushContext tracks:\n- `ProxyStatus`: Maps error codes to proxy IDs, for post-mortem debugging\n- `PushVersion`: Version string to detect stale proxy state\n- Per-resource generation errors and warnings\n- Performance metrics: InitContext time, resource generation time\n\n```go\nps.AddMetric(metric, key, proxyID, \"timeout generating CDS\")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Service Registry and Multi-Cluster Support\n\n### Overview\n\nThe Service Registry provides Pilot with a dynamic view of services and endpoints across one or more service discovery backends (Kubernetes, Consul, VM service entries). It's the foundation for EDS and notifies Pilot when endpoints change.\n\n**Source:**\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go` — Aggregate registry\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/` — Kubernetes controller\n- `pilot/pkg/model/config.go`, `pilot/pkg/model/service.go` — Service and endpoint abstractions\n\n### The Service Discovery Interface\n\n```go\ntype ServiceDiscovery interface {\n    // Get all services in the mesh\n    Services() []*Service\n\n    // Get all instances (endpoints) for a service port\n    InstancesByPort(svc *Service, port int, labels labels.Set) []*IstioEndpoint\n\n    // Get service information\n    GetService(hostname host.Name) *Service\n}\n```\n\n### Service Structure\n\n```go\ntype Service struct {\n    Hostname     host.Name                // e.g., \"reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n    Ports        []*Port                  // Service ports with protocol, target port\n    Addresses    []string                 // Cluster IPs / headless addresses\n    MeshExternal bool\n    SourceNamespace string\n    Resolution   Resolution               // \"DNS\" / \"STATIC\"\n    Attributes   ServiceAttributes\n}\n\ntype IstioEndpoint struct {\n    Labels       map[string]string        // Pod labels\n    Locality     *core.Locality           // Region/Zone\n    Address      string                   // IP address\n    Port         uint32\n    ServicePort  *Port                    // Reference to service port\n    Weight       uint32\n    TLSMode      string                   // \"ISTIO\" for mTLS\n}\n```\n\n### Kubernetes Service Registry\n\nThe Kubernetes provider watches:\n- **Services:** Create/update/delete events → `SvcUpdate()` (CDS)\n- **Endpoints/EndpointSlices:** Add/remove endpoints → `EDSUpdate()` (EDS)\n- **Pods:** Labels and status changes → `EDSUpdate()` for label-based grouping\n\n```go\n// Watches and triggering pushes\nfunc (c *Controller) ServiceHandler(ev config.Event) {\n    // SvcUpdate triggers full push with CDS + config changes\n    c.XDSUpdater.SvcUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, event)\n}\n\nfunc (c *Controller) EndpointHandler(ev config.Event) {\n    // EDSUpdate triggers incremental endpoint push\n    c.XDSUpdater.EDSUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, endpoints)\n}\n```\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go`\n\n### Aggregate Controller Pattern\n\nFor multi-registry support, the Aggregate Controller coordinates multiple service registries:\n\n```go\ntype Controller struct {\n    registries []*registryEntry      // Kubernetes cluster controllers + ServiceEntry registry\n    handlers   model.ControllerHandlers\n}\n\n// Services() aggregates across all registries\nfunc (c *Controller) Services() []*Service {\n    var allServices []*Service\n    for _, reg := range c.GetRegistries() {\n        allServices = append(allServices, reg.Services()...)\n    }\n    return allServices\n}\n```\n\nThis pattern enables:\n- **Multi-Cluster:** Each Kubernetes cluster is a separate registry\n- **Hybrid:** Kubernetes services + ServiceEntry-based services\n- **Layering:** Apply visibility rules, namespace scoping, etc.\n\n### Multi-Cluster Deployment\n\nIn a multi-cluster mesh:\n\n1. **Remote Cluster Registration:** Each remote cluster's services are discovered via:\n   - Kubernetes API server (if Pilot can access it)\n   - ServiceEntry resources created by Istio's **multiclusters-controller**\n\n2. **Endpoint Sharding:** Endpoints are grouped by cluster and shard:\n   ```go\n   type ShardKey struct {\n       Cluster    cluster.ID\n       Registry   provider.ID  // \"Kubernetes\", \"ServiceEntry\", etc.\n   }\n\n   // Multiple shards for the same service\n   // Example: reviews.default.svc.cluster.local has endpoints from cluster1 and cluster2\n   EndpointIndex[svc:port][shard] → []*IstioEndpoint\n   ```\n\n3. **EDS Aggregation:** When generating EDS, all endpoints from all clusters are aggregated:\n   ```go\n   func (ps *PushContext) getEdsInstances(svc *Service) []*IstioEndpoint {\n       var endpoints []*IstioEndpoint\n       for _, shards := range ps.EndpointIndex[svc.Key()] {\n           endpoints = append(endpoints, shards...)  // All clusters' endpoints\n       }\n       return endpoints\n   }\n   ```\n\n4. **Locality-Aware Load Balancing:** Envoy's locality-aware load balancing ensures local endpoints are preferred:\n   - Endpoints tagged with region/zone from Kubernetes node\n   - Failover to remote clusters if local unavailable\n\n### Service Registry Updates and Triggers\n\nThe `XDSUpdater` interface defines what triggers pushes:\n\n```go\ntype XDSUpdater interface {\n    // Full service definition changed\n    SvcUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, event Event)\n\n    // Service endpoints changed (incremental)\n    EDSUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, entry []*IstioEndpoint)\n\n    // Config (VirtualService, DestinationRule, etc.) changed\n    ConfigUpdate(req *PushRequest)\n}\n```\n\n**Push Triggers:**\n\n| Event | Push Type | Why |\n|-------|-----------|-----|\n| Service added | Full (CDS) | New clusters needed |\n| Service ports changed | Full (CDS) | Cluster definitions affected |\n| Endpoints added/removed | Incremental (EDS) | Load balancer pool changes |\n| Pod labels change | Incremental (EDS) | Same — affects endpoint grouping |\n| VirtualService changed | Full (RDS) | Route definitions affected |\n| DestinationRule changed | Full (CDS+RDS) | Policies + subset routing affected |\n| AuthorizationPolicy changed | Full (RDS) | May affect which routes apply |\n| ServiceEntry changed | Full (CDS+EDS) | Similar to service change |\n\n### Service Registry-to-EDS Data Flow\n\n```\nKubernetes API Server (Endpoints/Pods)\n    ↓\nController watches [Endpoints/EndpointSlices/Pods]\n    ↓\nbuildEndpointShards() [parse labels, assign localities]\n    ↓\nXDSUpdater.EDSUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, []*IstioEndpoint)\n    ↓\nPushContext.EndpointIndex[hostname][shard] = endpoints\n    ↓\nEDSGenerator.Generate(proxy)\n    ├─→ For each watched service in proxy's sidecar scope\n    ├─→ Fetch endpoints from PushContext.EndpointIndex\n    ├─→ Apply subset selection (DestinationRule)\n    ├─→ Apply load balancer config (DestinationRule)\n    ├─→ Build ClusterLoadAssignment (Envoy protobuf)\n    ↓\nSend via xDS to all proxies\n```\n\n### Extension Points in Service Registry\n\n1. **Custom Registries:** Implement `ServiceDiscovery` interface to add new backends\n2. **ServiceEntry Resources:** Define services not in Kubernetes (VMs, external services)\n3. **WorkloadEntry:** Register VMs with full pod-like capabilities (labels, health checks)\n4. **Multi-Cluster:** Istiod in primary cluster reads from remote clusters via Kubernetes API\n\n---\n\n## Data Flow: Config Change to xDS Push\n\nHere's the end-to-end path when an Istio VirtualService is created:\n\n```\n1. User applies VirtualService YAML\n   ↓\n2. Kubernetes API Server persists it\n   ↓\n3. Pilot's config watcher [in ConfigStore] detects the change\n   ↓\n4. ConfigUpdate() called with PushRequest{ConfigsUpdated: {VirtualService key}}\n   ↓\n5. pushChannel receives the request (non-blocking, async)\n   ↓\n6. handleUpdates() goroutine debounces for 100ms\n   ↓\n7. Push() called with debounced PushRequest\n   ↓\n8. initPushContext() called\n   ├─→ createNewContext() OR updateContext()\n   ├─→ initVirtualServices(env)\n   │   ├─→ virtualServiceIndex rebuilt\n   │   └─→ Index contains all VS with their routes/destinations\n   ├─→ initSidecarScopes(env)  [may rebuild if routing changed]\n   └─→ Returned PushContext fully initialized\n   ↓\n9. AdsPushAll(PushRequest) called\n   ├─→ For each Connection in adsClients\n   └─→ pushQueue.Enqueue(conn, pushRequest)\n   ↓\n10. sendPushes() goroutine (respects concurrentPushLimit)\n    ├─→ Dequeue conn + pushRequest from pushQueue\n    ├─→ Send Event to conn.PushCh()\n    ↓\n11. Connection.Push() deserializes the event\n    ├─→ s.pushConnection(conn, event)\n    ├─→ For each watched resource type (CDS, RDS, LDS, EDS)\n    │   ├─→ Fetch/generate from cache or call Generator\n    │   └─→ RDSGenerator.Generate(proxy, pushRequest) called\n    │       ├─→ Use PushContext.virtualServiceIndex to find relevant VS\n    │       ├─→ Use PushContext.destinationRuleIndex for policies\n    │       ├─→ Use proxy.SidecarScope to filter destinations\n    │       └─→ Build RouteConfiguration (Envoy protobuf)\n    └─→ Send DiscoveryResponse with new routes\n    ↓\n12. Envoy receives RDS update\n    ├─→ Validates and loads new RouteConfiguration\n    └─→ Routes traffic according to new VirtualService rules\n```\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### At Each Stage\n\n**Config Validation (PushContext.InitContext)**\n- Validation errors recorded in `ProxyStatus`\n- Push continues; affected proxies receive best-effort configuration\n- Errors visible in debug endpoints: `/debug/adsz`, `/debug/config_dump`\n\n**Push Generation (Generators)**\n- Resource generation errors caught and logged per proxy\n- Partial responses sent when possible\n- `ProxyStatus` updated with error code and proxy ID\n\n**Proxy Disconnection**\n- `closeConnection()` removes from `adsClients`\n- Push operations check stream context; send fails gracefully\n- State cleaned up; workload auto-registration notified\n\n**Network Failures**\n- gRPC stream context cancellation triggers connection cleanup\n- Proxy must reconnect; Pilot doesn't maintain retry logic\n\n---\n\n## Summary Table: Component Responsibilities\n\n| Component | Responsibility | Key Files |\n|-----------|-----------------|-----------|\n| **DiscoveryServer** | gRPC server, debouncing, concurrency control, push coordination | `xds/discovery.go` |\n| **ADS (Stream Handler)** | Connection lifecycle, request processing, push serialization | `xds/ads.go` |\n| **Connection** | Proxy metadata, watched resources, push channel | `xds/ads.go` |\n| **PushContext** | Config snapshot, routing indexes, translation output | `model/push_context.go` |\n| **ServiceRegistry** | Service discovery, endpoint tracking, change notification | `serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go` |\n| **Resource Generators** | Translate PushContext to Envoy resources (CDS, RDS, LDS, EDS) | `xds/cds.go`, `xds/eds.go`, `networking/core/route.go` |\n\n---\n\n## Key Insights\n\n1. **Immutability:** PushContext is immutable once created. All proxies in a push cycle use the same snapshot, ensuring consistency.\n\n2. **Decoupling:** Config changes are decoupled from actual push operations via debouncing and the push queue. High-frequency events don't overwhelm Envoy.\n\n3. **Incremental Updates:** Full pushes rebuild PushContext, but incremental EDS pushes reuse the old context, making scaling possible.\n\n4. **Extensibility:** Custom generators per resource type and proxy metadata allow for advanced use cases (traffic engineering, canary deployments, cross-mesh federation).\n\n5. **Multi-Cluster:** Service aggregation happens transparently; generators work with `ServiceIndex` that includes all clusters, making multi-cluster \"just work.\"\n\n6. **Push Isolation:** Each proxy's push happens independently via `Connection.Push()`. Failures in one proxy's generation don't block others.\n\n7. **Observability:** Push metrics, proxy status, and debug endpoints provide visibility into the push pipeline and troubleshooting.\n\n---\n\n## Relevant Source Files\n\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` — DiscoveryServer main logic\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go` — ADS stream handler and Connection\n- `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go` — PushContext and initialization\n- `pilot/pkg/model/context.go` — Environment and Proxy definitions\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go` — Aggregate registry\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go` — Kubernetes service controller\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go` — Cluster (CDS) resource generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go` — Endpoint (EDS) resource generator\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/route/route.go` — Route (RDS) resource generator\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/cluster.go` — Cluster building logic\n- `pilot/pkg/features/xds.go` — Feature flags (debounce, push throttle, caching)\n- `pilot/pkg/bootstrap/discovery.go` — Server initialization\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1494,"cache_read_input_tokens":54403,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1494},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"1f2345b9-3411-4f7e-bb0b-65e432ea3e99","uuid":"9eb61edd-6f0d-4473-988c-005c25998140"}

Pilot translates high-level Istio networking resources (VirtualServices, DestinationRules, Sidecars, etc.) into Envoy-specific configurations (Clusters, Routes, Listeners, Endpoints) and maintains a fleet-wide view of services across multiple Kubernetes clusters.\n\nThis document explains the architecture of four core subsystems:\n\n1. **DiscoveryServer** — Pilot's gRPC server implementing Envoy's xDS protocol\n2. **ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service)** — The bidirectional stream handler managing individual proxy connections\n3. **PushContext** — The immutable configuration snapshot used during a push cycle\n4. **Service Registry** — The service discovery layer integrating Kubernetes and multi-cluster data\n\n---\n\n## 1. DiscoveryServer — The xDS gRPC Server\n\n### Overview\n\nThe `DiscoveryServer` is Pilot's core gRPC server that implements Envoy's xDS v3 protocol. It serves as the central hub for pushing configuration changes to all connected proxies, managing client connections, and coordinating the push pipeline.\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`\n\n### Key Responsibilities\n\n- **gRPC Protocol Implementation:** Registers as an `AggregatedDiscoveryServiceServer` (v3) and handles bidirectional xDS streams\n- **Client Connection Management:** Tracks active proxy connections in `adsClients` map (keyed by connection ID)\n- **Push Coordination:** Debounces configuration changes, enforces rate limits, and serializes concurrent pushes\n- **Cache Management:** Maintains an `XdsCache` for generated xDS resources to avoid recomputation\n- **Readiness Enforcement:** Ensures all caches are synced before accepting client connections\n\n### Initialization\n\n```go\n// Created with environment and cluster aliases\nds := NewDiscoveryServer(env *model.Environment, clusterAliases map[string]string, debugger *krt.DebugHandler)\n```\n\nThe `DiscoveryServer` initializes with:\n- `Env`: The Istio environment containing service registry, config store, and push context\n- `Generators`: Map of custom `XdsResourceGenerator` implementations (extensible per resource type or per client)\n- `ProxyNeedsPush`: Optional filter function to skip pushes for specific proxies\n- `concurrentPushLimit`: Semaphore limiting concurrent push operations (controlled by `PILOT_PUSH_THROTTLE`)\n- `RequestRateLimit`: Rate limiter preventing thundering herd of incoming requests\n- `DebounceOptions`: Configuration for debouncing and merging rapid updates\n- `Cache`: XDS resource cache (optional, controlled by `PILOT_ENABLE_XDS_CACHE`)\n\n### The Push Pipeline\n\nWhen Istio configuration changes, the push follows this pipeline:\n\n```\nConfig Change Event\n    ↓\nConfigUpdate() [non-blocking, enqueued to pushChannel]\n    ↓\nhandleUpdates() goroutine [debouncing + merging]\n    ↓\nPush() [full or incremental]\n    ├─→ initPushContext() [rebuild config snapshot if full push]\n    ├─→ dropCacheForRequest() [clear affected cache entries]\n    ├─→ AdsPushAll() [enqueue to pushQueue for all proxies]\n    ↓\nsendPushes() goroutine [process pushQueue with concurrency limits]\n    ├─→ PushCh() [send Event to each connection's push channel]\n    ↓\nConnection.Push() [serialize per-connection push logic]\n```\n\n### Debouncing and Rate Control\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` - `debounce()` function\n\nThe discovery server implements two layers of debouncing:\n\n1. **Event Debouncing** (`handleUpdates`)\n   - Groups rapid configuration events within `DebounceAfter` window (default 100ms)\n   - Merges multiple events into a single `PushRequest`\n   - Enforces maximum delay of `debounceMax` (default 10s) to prevent indefinite delays\n   - Special handling for EDS (Endpoint Discovery Service) updates, which can bypass debouncing if `enableEDSDebounce` is false\n\n2. **Push Concurrency Control**\n   - `concurrentPushLimit` semaphore restricts simultaneous xDS push operations (default: 100)\n   - Prevents overwhelming the system with too many concurrent computations\n   - `RequestRateLimit` (rate limiter) throttles incoming xDS requests per second\n\n### Cache Management\n\nThe `Cache` field holds the XDS resource cache, implemented as:\n- `TypedXdsCache`: Maps (proxy metadata, resource type) → generated resource\n- Cleared selectively on config changes via `dropCacheForRequest()`\n- Fully cleared on forced/unknown updates\n- Accessed during resource generation to avoid recomputation\n\n### Metrics and Monitoring\n\nThe DiscoveryServer tracks:\n- `InboundUpdates`: Total config updates received\n- `CommittedUpdates`: Updates incorporated into the push context (subset of inbound)\n- Push times, debounce delays, queue depths\n- Per-proxy push status and errors (stored in `PushContext.ProxyStatus`)\n- Periodic metrics refresh every 10 seconds\n\n### Lifecycle\n\n```go\n// Startup\nserver.Start(stopCh <-chan struct{})\n    ├─→ WorkloadEntryController.Run()    // handle auto-registered workloads\n    ├─→ handleUpdates()                   // debounce config changes\n    ├─→ periodicRefreshMetrics()          // refresh push metrics\n    ├─→ sendPushes()                      // process push queue\n    └─→ Cache.Run()                       // background cache cleanup\n\n// Readiness\nserver.CachesSynced()  // called when all config stores are synced\nserver.IsServerReady() // checked before accepting connections\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. ADS and the Connection Model\n\n### Overview\n\nThe Aggregated Discovery Service (ADS) is Pilot's implementation of Envoy's bidirectional streaming gRPC protocol. Each connected proxy maintains a persistent stream with Pilot, and ADS coordinates what configuration gets pushed to each proxy individually.\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`\n\n### The Connection Type\n\n```go\ntype Connection struct {\n    xds.Connection\n    node       *core.Node                    // Original Envoy node metadata\n    proxy      *model.Proxy                  // Parsed proxy metadata\n    deltaStream DeltaDiscoveryStream         // For delta/incremental mode\n    stream     DiscoveryStream                // For state-of-world mode\n    s          *DiscoveryServer\n    ids        []string                      // Auth identities\n}\n```\n\nThe `Connection` wraps the gRPC stream with:\n- **Proxy Metadata:** The `Proxy` object contains workload labels, locality, service targets, sidecar scope\n- **Stream Type:** Either `stream` (state-of-the-world) or `deltaStream` (incremental delta mode)\n- **Request Channel:** Buffered channel for push events from DiscoveryServer\n\n### Connection Lifecycle\n\n#### 1. Stream Establishment (`Stream()`)\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) Stream(stream xds.DiscoveryStream) error {\n    // Check server readiness\n    if !s.IsServerReady() {\n        return Unavailable error\n    }\n\n    // Rate limit enforcement\n    if err := s.WaitForRequestLimit(...); err != nil {\n        return ResourceExhausted error\n    }\n\n    // Authentication\n    ids, err := s.authenticate(stream.Context())\n\n    // Initialize push context if needed\n    s.globalPushContext().InitContext(...)\n\n    // Create connection wrapper\n    conn := newConnection(peerAddr, stream)\n    conn.s = s\n    conn.ids = ids\n\n    // Delegate to xds.Stream (handles stream I/O loop)\n    return xds.Stream(conn)\n}\n```\n\nThe stream handling is delegated to the `xds.Stream()` function from the `go-control-plane` library, which manages the gRPC stream's read/write loops while calling into our `Connection` methods for protocol handling.\n\n#### 2. Connection Initialization (`initConnection()`)\n\nWhen the first discovery request arrives (containing node metadata), Pilot initializes the proxy:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) initConnection(node *core.Node, con *Connection, identities []string) error {\n    // Parse node metadata and create Proxy object\n    proxy, err := s.initProxyMetadata(node)\n\n    // Apply cluster aliases (for multi-cluster scenarios)\n    if alias, exists := s.ClusterAliases[proxy.Metadata.ClusterID]; exists {\n        proxy.Metadata.ClusterID = alias\n    }\n\n    // Capture current push context as baseline for this proxy\n    proxy.LastPushContext = s.globalPushContext()\n\n    // Assign connection ID\n    con.SetID(connectionID(proxy.ID))\n\n    // Authorize proxy\n    if err := s.authorize(con, identities); err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n\n    // Register connection (enables push targeting)\n    s.addCon(con.ID(), con)\n    defer con.MarkInitialized()\n\n    // Full initialization: compute sidecar scope, service targets, security policies\n    return s.initializeProxy(con)\n}\n```\n\n**Key Steps:**\n- **Metadata Parsing:** Extract cluster, namespace, workload labels from node metadata\n- **Cluster Alias Resolution:** Support for multi-cluster alias names\n- **Baseline PushContext:** Capture the current push context to ensure this proxy doesn't receive older pushes\n- **Registration:** Add to `adsClients` map to enable future push targeting\n- **Proxy Initialization:** Expensive computation like sidecar scope lookup happens here\n\n#### 3. Connection Shutdown (`closeConnection()`)\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) closeConnection(con *Connection) {\n    s.removeCon(con.ID())\n    s.WorkloadEntryController.OnDisconnect(con)\n}\n```\n\nRemoves the connection from the tracking map and notifies the workload entry controller (for auto-registration cleanup).\n\n### Request Processing\n\n#### `processRequest(req *DiscoveryRequest, con *Connection)`\n\nWhen a proxy sends a discovery request, Pilot determines which resources to send back:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) processRequest(req *DiscoveryRequest, con *Connection) error {\n    stype := v3.GetShortType(req.TypeUrl)  // e.g., \"CDS\" from cluster type URL\n\n    // Debug endpoints bypass normal processing\n    if strings.HasPrefix(req.TypeUrl, v3.DebugType) {\n        return s.pushXds(con, req.TypeUrl, ...)\n    }\n\n    // Update tracked watched resources\n    con.UpdateWatchedResource(req)\n\n    // Determine if proxy needs this push\n    if needsPush := computeNeedsPush(req, con); !needsPush {\n        return nil  // Skip if already satisfied\n    }\n\n    // Fetch or generate resources\n    return s.pushXds(con, req.TypeUrl, ...)\n}\n```\n\n**Resource Type Handling:** Pilot handles multiple xDS resource types:\n- **CDS (Cluster Discovery Service):** Envoy cluster configurations (load balancing, circuit breakers)\n- **RDS (Route Discovery Service):** HTTP route configurations\n- **LDS (Listener Discovery Service):** Envoy listeners (inbound/outbound)\n- **EDS (Endpoint Discovery Service):** Service endpoint instances\n\n#### Push to Connection (`pushConnection()`)\n\nWhen a push is triggered, all relevant proxies receive updates via `pushConnection()`:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) pushConnection(con *Connection, ev *Event) error {\n    pushReq := ev.pushRequest\n\n    // Early filter: skip if proxy doesn't need this push\n    if filteredReq, ok := s.ProxyNeedsPush(con.proxy, pushReq); !ok {\n        return nil\n    }\n\n    // For each watched resource type\n    for typeUrl, watchedRes := range con.proxy.WatchedResources {\n        // Generate or fetch resources\n        res, logDetails, err := s.generateResources(con.proxy, typeUrl, filteredReq)\n\n        // Send response\n        response := &DiscoveryResponse{\n            TypeUrl:     typeUrl,\n            Resources:   res,\n            VersionInfo: generateVersionString(),\n            Nonce:       nonce(\"push\"),\n        }\n        con.Send(response)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### StartPush and Fleet-Wide Updates\n\nThe `AdsPushAll()` method initiates a fleet-wide push:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) AdsPushAll(req *model.PushRequest) {\n    s.adsClientsMutex.RLock()\n    for id, conn := range s.adsClients {\n        // Enqueue push for each proxy\n        s.pushQueue.Enqueue(conn, req)\n    }\n    s.adsClientsMutex.RUnlock()\n}\n```\n\nThis is non-blocking; the actual serialization happens in `sendPushes()` goroutine, which reads from `pushQueue` and respects the `concurrentPushLimit`.\n\n---\n\n## 3. PushContext — Configuration Snapshot and Translation\n\n### Overview\n\n`PushContext` is an immutable snapshot of all Istio configuration, services, and security policies at a point in time. It's computed once per push cycle and shared across all proxy generations to ensure consistency.\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`\n\n### What PushContext Holds\n\n```go\ntype PushContext struct {\n    // Service information\n    ServiceIndex serviceIndex          // Services indexed by namespace, host, and visibility\n    serviceAccounts map[key][]string   // Service account mappings\n\n    // Routing configuration\n    virtualServiceIndex virtualServiceIndex    // Virtual services indexed by gateway/namespace\n    destinationRuleIndex destinationRuleIndex  // Destination rules (traffic policies)\n\n    // Ingress and gateway configuration\n    gatewayIndex gatewayIndex         // Kubernetes gateways and Istio gateways\n\n    // Policy and extension configuration\n    AuthnPolicies *AuthenticationPolicies      // RequestAuthentication, PeerAuthentication\n    AuthzPolicies *AuthorizationPolicies       // AuthorizationPolicy rules\n    envoyFiltersByNamespace map[string][]*EnvoyFilterWrapper\n    wasmPluginsByNamespace map[string][]*WasmPluginWrapper\n    Telemetry *Telemetries            // Telemetry (traces, metrics, logs)\n    ProxyConfigs *ProxyConfigs         // ProxyConfig resources\n\n    // Network configuration\n    Mesh *meshconfig.MeshConfig        // Global mesh settings\n    Networks *meshconfig.MeshNetworks  // Multi-cluster network definitions\n    networkMgr *NetworkManager         // Gateway addresses per network\n\n    // Sidecar scoping\n    sidecarIndex sidecarIndex          // Workload-specific sidecar rules\n\n    // Metrics and status\n    ProxyStatus map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus\n    PushVersion string                 // Version identifier for this push\n\n    // Ambient support\n    ambientIndex AmbientIndexes        // Ambient mesh specific indexes\n\n    // Caching and resolution\n    JwtKeyResolver *JwksResolver       // JWKS public key resolver\n    GatewayAPIController GatewayController  // Gateway API resources\n}\n```\n\n### InitContext — Building the Snapshot\n\nWhen a full push is triggered, `initPushContext()` builds a new `PushContext`:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) initPushContext(req *model.PushRequest, oldPushContext *model.PushContext, version string) *model.PushContext {\n    push := model.NewPushContext()\n    push.PushVersion = version\n\n    // InitContext does the actual work\n    push.InitContext(s.Env, oldPushContext, req)\n    return push\n}\n```\n\nThe `InitContext()` method executes initialization in two paths:\n\n#### Full Context Creation\n\nIf no previous context exists or the update is forced:\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) createNewContext(env *Environment) {\n    ps.initServiceRegistry(env, nil)      // Load all services\n    ps.initKubernetesGateways(env)        // Load K8s Gateway API resources\n    ps.initVirtualServices(env)            // Index virtual services\n    ps.initDestinationRules(env)           // Index destination rules and traffic policies\n    ps.initAuthnPolicies(env)              // Load authentication policies\n    ps.initAuthorizationPolicies(env)      // Load authorization policies\n    ps.initTelemetry(env)                  // Load telemetry configurations\n    ps.initProxyConfigs(env)               // Load proxy configurations\n    ps.initWasmPlugins(env)                // Load WASM plugins\n    ps.initEnvoyFilters(env, nil, nil)     // Load Envoy filter patches\n    ps.initGateways(env)                   // Index gateways\n    ps.initAmbient(env)                    // Initialize ambient mesh indexes\n    ps.initSidecarScopes(env)              // Compute workload sidecar scopes (must be last)\n}\n```\n\n#### Incremental Context Update\n\nFor faster incremental updates, only changed configuration is recomputed:\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) updateContext(env *Environment, oldPushContext *model.PushContext, pushReq *model.PushRequest) {\n    // Analyze what changed\n    for conf := range pushReq.ConfigsUpdated {\n        switch conf.Kind {\n        case kind.ServiceEntry, kind.DNSName:\n            servicesChanged = true\n        case kind.VirtualService:\n            virtualServicesChanged = true\n        case kind.DestinationRule:\n            destinationRulesChanged = true\n        // ... other config types\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Recompute only affected parts\n    if servicesChanged {\n        ps.initServiceRegistry(env, pushReq.ConfigsUpdated)\n    } else {\n        ps.ServiceIndex = oldPushContext.ServiceIndex\n    }\n\n    if virtualServicesChanged {\n        ps.initVirtualServices(env)\n    } else {\n        ps.virtualServiceIndex = oldPushContext.virtualServiceIndex\n    }\n    // ... similar for other resources\n\n    // Sidecar scopes may need recomputation if services/routing changed\n    if servicesChanged || virtualServicesChanged || destinationRulesChanged || sidecarsChanged {\n        ps.initSidecarScopes(env)\n    } else {\n        ps.sidecarIndex = oldPushContext.sidecarIndex\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThis optimization is crucial for scalability — most pushes are incremental EDS updates that don't require rebuilding the entire routing configuration.\n\n### Configuration Translation: Istio → Envoy\n\nThe `PushContext` is then used by resource generators to translate Istio resources into Envoy configurations. The translation happens in two stages:\n\n#### 1. Service Registry to EDS\n\nWhen services or endpoints change, the registry triggers EDS (Endpoint Discovery Service) updates:\n\n```\nK8s Service/Pod Change\n    ↓\nServiceRegistry.WorkItem() [watches K8s resources]\n    ↓\nXDSUpdater.EDSUpdate() [or SvcUpdate()]\n    ↓\nConfigUpdate(PushRequest{Full: false}) [incremental EDS push]\n    ↓\nEDS Generator generates() [endpoints from ServiceIndex]\n```\n\n#### 2. VirtualService + DestinationRule to CDS/RDS\n\nPilot translates Istio's routing policies into Envoy clusters and routes:\n\n- **VirtualService** → Envoy **RouteConfiguration** (RDS)\n  - Routes matching on HTTP host/path to destination clusters\n  - Retries, timeouts, traffic shifting\n\n- **DestinationRule** → Envoy **Cluster** modifications (CDS)\n  - Load balancer policy, outlier detection\n  - TLS settings, connection pooling\n\n- **VirtualService** + **DestinationRule** + **DestinationRule subsets** → Multiple **Clusters** per destination\n\n**Source Code:**\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/cluster.go` — Cluster (CDS) generation\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/route/route.go` — Route (RDS) generation\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/cluster_builder.go` — Cluster building from Istio resources\n\n#### 3. Sidecar Scope Filtering\n\nFor each proxy, the `SidecarScope` (from the Sidecar resource) determines:\n- Which services are reachable from this workload\n- Which inbound/outbound listeners to create\n- Which traffic policies apply\n\n```go\n// Computed during InitContext\nsidecarScope := ps.GetSidecarScope(proxy)\n\n// Used during resource generation\nif !sidecarScope.IsVisible(service) {\n    return  // Skip this service in CDS/RDS for this proxy\n}\n```\n\n### Extension Points in PushContext\n\n1. **Custom Generators:** The `Generators` map in `DiscoveryServer` can override resource generation per proxy type or resource type\n2. **ProxyNeedsPush Filter:** Custom logic to skip pushes for certain proxies\n3. **Telemetry Plugins:** Extensions in `Telemetry` configuration\n4. **WASM Plugins:** Extensions specified in `WasmPlugin` resources\n5. **EnvoyFilter Patches:** Customize generated Envoy configuration via patches\n\n### Metrics and Error Tracking\n\nPushContext tracks:\n- `ProxyStatus`: Maps error codes to proxy IDs, for post-mortem debugging\n- `PushVersion`: Version string to detect stale proxy state\n- Per-resource generation errors and warnings\n- Performance metrics: InitContext time, resource generation time\n\n```go\nps.AddMetric(metric, key, proxyID, \"timeout generating CDS\")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Service Registry and Multi-Cluster Support\n\n### Overview\n\nThe Service Registry provides Pilot with a dynamic view of services and endpoints across one or more service discovery backends (Kubernetes, Consul, VM service entries). It's the foundation for EDS and notifies Pilot when endpoints change.\n\n**Source:**\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go` — Aggregate registry\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/` — Kubernetes controller\n- `pilot/pkg/model/config.go`, `pilot/pkg/model/service.go` — Service and endpoint abstractions\n\n### The Service Discovery Interface\n\n```go\ntype ServiceDiscovery interface {\n    // Get all services in the mesh\n    Services() []*Service\n\n    // Get all instances (endpoints) for a service port\n    InstancesByPort(svc *Service, port int, labels labels.Set) []*IstioEndpoint\n\n    // Get service information\n    GetService(hostname host.Name) *Service\n}\n```\n\n### Service Structure\n\n```go\ntype Service struct {\n    Hostname     host.Name                // e.g., \"reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n    Ports        []*Port                  // Service ports with protocol, target port\n    Addresses    []string                 // Cluster IPs / headless addresses\n    MeshExternal bool\n    SourceNamespace string\n    Resolution   Resolution               // \"DNS\" / \"STATIC\"\n    Attributes   ServiceAttributes\n}\n\ntype IstioEndpoint struct {\n    Labels       map[string]string        // Pod labels\n    Locality     *core.Locality           // Region/Zone\n    Address      string                   // IP address\n    Port         uint32\n    ServicePort  *Port                    // Reference to service port\n    Weight       uint32\n    TLSMode      string                   // \"ISTIO\" for mTLS\n}\n```\n\n### Kubernetes Service Registry\n\nThe Kubernetes provider watches:\n- **Services:** Create/update/delete events → `SvcUpdate()` (CDS)\n- **Endpoints/EndpointSlices:** Add/remove endpoints → `EDSUpdate()` (EDS)\n- **Pods:** Labels and status changes → `EDSUpdate()` for label-based grouping\n\n```go\n// Watches and triggering pushes\nfunc (c *Controller) ServiceHandler(ev config.Event) {\n    // SvcUpdate triggers full push with CDS + config changes\n    c.XDSUpdater.SvcUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, event)\n}\n\nfunc (c *Controller) EndpointHandler(ev config.Event) {\n    // EDSUpdate triggers incremental endpoint push\n    c.XDSUpdater.EDSUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, endpoints)\n}\n```\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go`\n\n### Aggregate Controller Pattern\n\nFor multi-registry support, the Aggregate Controller coordinates multiple service registries:\n\n```go\ntype Controller struct {\n    registries []*registryEntry      // Kubernetes cluster controllers + ServiceEntry registry\n    handlers   model.ControllerHandlers\n}\n\n// Services() aggregates across all registries\nfunc (c *Controller) Services() []*Service {\n    var allServices []*Service\n    for _, reg := range c.GetRegistries() {\n        allServices = append(allServices, reg.Services()...)\n    }\n    return allServices\n}\n```\n\nThis pattern enables:\n- **Multi-Cluster:** Each Kubernetes cluster is a separate registry\n- **Hybrid:** Kubernetes services + ServiceEntry-based services\n- **Layering:** Apply visibility rules, namespace scoping, etc.\n\n### Multi-Cluster Deployment\n\nIn a multi-cluster mesh:\n\n1. **Remote Cluster Registration:** Each remote cluster's services are discovered via:\n   - Kubernetes API server (if Pilot can access it)\n   - ServiceEntry resources created by Istio's **multiclusters-controller**\n\n2. **Endpoint Sharding:** Endpoints are grouped by cluster and shard:\n   ```go\n   type ShardKey struct {\n       Cluster    cluster.ID\n       Registry   provider.ID  // \"Kubernetes\", \"ServiceEntry\", etc.\n   }\n\n   // Multiple shards for the same service\n   // Example: reviews.default.svc.cluster.local has endpoints from cluster1 and cluster2\n   EndpointIndex[svc:port][shard] → []*IstioEndpoint\n   ```\n\n3. **EDS Aggregation:** When generating EDS, all endpoints from all clusters are aggregated:\n   ```go\n   func (ps *PushContext) getEdsInstances(svc *Service) []*IstioEndpoint {\n       var endpoints []*IstioEndpoint\n       for _, shards := range ps.EndpointIndex[svc.Key()] {\n           endpoints = append(endpoints, shards...)  // All clusters' endpoints\n       }\n       return endpoints\n   }\n   ```\n\n4. **Locality-Aware Load Balancing:** Envoy's locality-aware load balancing ensures local endpoints are preferred:\n   - Endpoints tagged with region/zone from Kubernetes node\n   - Failover to remote clusters if local unavailable\n\n### Service Registry Updates and Triggers\n\nThe `XDSUpdater` interface defines what triggers pushes:\n\n```go\ntype XDSUpdater interface {\n    // Full service definition changed\n    SvcUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, event Event)\n\n    // Service endpoints changed (incremental)\n    EDSUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, entry []*IstioEndpoint)\n\n    // Config (VirtualService, DestinationRule, etc.) changed\n    ConfigUpdate(req *PushRequest)\n}\n```\n\n**Push Triggers:**\n\n| Event | Push Type | Why |\n|-------|-----------|-----|\n| Service added | Full (CDS) | New clusters needed |\n| Service ports changed | Full (CDS) | Cluster definitions affected |\n| Endpoints added/removed | Incremental (EDS) | Load balancer pool changes |\n| Pod labels change | Incremental (EDS) | Same — affects endpoint grouping |\n| VirtualService changed | Full (RDS) | Route definitions affected |\n| DestinationRule changed | Full (CDS+RDS) | Policies + subset routing affected |\n| AuthorizationPolicy changed | Full (RDS) | May affect which routes apply |\n| ServiceEntry changed | Full (CDS+EDS) | Similar to service change |\n\n### Service Registry-to-EDS Data Flow\n\n```\nKubernetes API Server (Endpoints/Pods)\n    ↓\nController watches [Endpoints/EndpointSlices/Pods]\n    ↓\nbuildEndpointShards() [parse labels, assign localities]\n    ↓\nXDSUpdater.EDSUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, []*IstioEndpoint)\n    ↓\nPushContext.EndpointIndex[hostname][shard] = endpoints\n    ↓\nEDSGenerator.Generate(proxy)\n    ├─→ For each watched service in proxy's sidecar scope\n    ├─→ Fetch endpoints from PushContext.EndpointIndex\n    ├─→ Apply subset selection (DestinationRule)\n    ├─→ Apply load balancer config (DestinationRule)\n    ├─→ Build ClusterLoadAssignment (Envoy protobuf)\n    ↓\nSend via xDS to all proxies\n```\n\n### Extension Points in Service Registry\n\n1. **Custom Registries:** Implement `ServiceDiscovery` interface to add new backends\n2. **ServiceEntry Resources:** Define services not in Kubernetes (VMs, external services)\n3. **WorkloadEntry:** Register VMs with full pod-like capabilities (labels, health checks)\n4. **Multi-Cluster:** Istiod in primary cluster reads from remote clusters via Kubernetes API\n\n---\n\n## Data Flow: Config Change to xDS Push\n\nHere's the end-to-end path when an Istio VirtualService is created:\n\n```\n1. User applies VirtualService YAML\n   ↓\n2. Kubernetes API Server persists it\n   ↓\n3. Pilot's config watcher [in ConfigStore] detects the change\n   ↓\n4. ConfigUpdate() called with PushRequest{ConfigsUpdated: {VirtualService key}}\n   ↓\n5. pushChannel receives the request (non-blocking, async)\n   ↓\n6. handleUpdates() goroutine debounces for 100ms\n   ↓\n7. Push() called with debounced PushRequest\n   ↓\n8. initPushContext() called\n   ├─→ createNewContext() OR updateContext()\n   ├─→ initVirtualServices(env)\n   │   ├─→ virtualServiceIndex rebuilt\n   │   └─→ Index contains all VS with their routes/destinations\n   ├─→ initSidecarScopes(env)  [may rebuild if routing changed]\n   └─→ Returned PushContext fully initialized\n   ↓\n9. AdsPushAll(PushRequest) called\n   ├─→ For each Connection in adsClients\n   └─→ pushQueue.Enqueue(conn, pushRequest)\n   ↓\n10. sendPushes() goroutine (respects concurrentPushLimit)\n    ├─→ Dequeue conn + pushRequest from pushQueue\n    ├─→ Send Event to conn.PushCh()\n    ↓\n11. Connection.Push() deserializes the event\n    ├─→ s.pushConnection(conn, event)\n    ├─→ For each watched resource type (CDS, RDS, LDS, EDS)\n    │   ├─→ Fetch/generate from cache or call Generator\n    │   └─→ RDSGenerator.Generate(proxy, pushRequest) called\n    │       ├─→ Use PushContext.virtualServiceIndex to find relevant VS\n    │       ├─→ Use PushContext.destinationRuleIndex for policies\n    │       ├─→ Use proxy.SidecarScope to filter destinations\n    │       └─→ Build RouteConfiguration (Envoy protobuf)\n    └─→ Send DiscoveryResponse with new routes\n    ↓\n12. Envoy receives RDS update\n    ├─→ Validates and loads new RouteConfiguration\n    └─→ Routes traffic according to new VirtualService rules\n```\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### At Each Stage\n\n**Config Validation (PushContext.InitContext)**\n- Validation errors recorded in `ProxyStatus`\n- Push continues; affected proxies receive best-effort configuration\n- Errors visible in debug endpoints: `/debug/adsz`, `/debug/config_dump`\n\n**Push Generation (Generators)**\n- Resource generation errors caught and logged per proxy\n- Partial responses sent when possible\n- `ProxyStatus` updated with error code and proxy ID\n\n**Proxy Disconnection**\n- `closeConnection()` removes from `adsClients`\n- Push operations check stream context; send fails gracefully\n- State cleaned up; workload auto-registration notified\n\n**Network Failures**\n- gRPC stream context cancellation triggers connection cleanup\n- Proxy must reconnect; Pilot doesn't maintain retry logic\n\n---\n\n## Summary Table: Component Responsibilities\n\n| Component | Responsibility | Key Files |\n|-----------|-----------------|-----------|\n| **DiscoveryServer** | gRPC server, debouncing, concurrency control, push coordination | `xds/discovery.go` |\n| **ADS (Stream Handler)** | Connection lifecycle, request processing, push serialization | `xds/ads.go` |\n| **Connection** | Proxy metadata, watched resources, push channel | `xds/ads.go` |\n| **PushContext** | Config snapshot, routing indexes, translation output | `model/push_context.go` |\n| **ServiceRegistry** | Service discovery, endpoint tracking, change notification | `serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go` |\n| **Resource Generators** | Translate PushContext to Envoy resources (CDS, RDS, LDS, EDS) | `xds/cds.go`, `xds/eds.go`, `networking/core/route.go` |\n\n---\n\n## Key Insights\n\n1. **Immutability:** PushContext is immutable once created. All proxies in a push cycle use the same snapshot, ensuring consistency.\n\n2. **Decoupling:** Config changes are decoupled from actual push operations via debouncing and the push queue. High-frequency events don't overwhelm Envoy.\n\n3. **Incremental Updates:** Full pushes rebuild PushContext, but incremental EDS pushes reuse the old context, making scaling possible.\n\n4. **Extensibility:** Custom generators per resource type and proxy metadata allow for advanced use cases (traffic engineering, canary deployments, cross-mesh federation).\n\n5. **Multi-Cluster:** Service aggregation happens transparently; generators work with `ServiceIndex` that includes all clusters, making multi-cluster \"just work.\"\n\n6. **Push Isolation:** Each proxy's push happens independently via `Connection.Push()`. Failures in one proxy's generation don't block others.\n\n7. **Observability:** Push metrics, proxy status, and debug endpoints provide visibility into the push pipeline and troubleshooting.\n\n---\n\n## Relevant Source Files\n\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` — DiscoveryServer main logic\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go` — ADS stream handler and Connection\n- `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go` — PushContext and initialization\n- `pilot/pkg/model/context.go` — Environment and Proxy definitions\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go` — Aggregate registry\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go` — Kubernetes service controller\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go` — Cluster (CDS) resource generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go` — Endpoint (EDS) resource generator\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/route/route.go` — Route (RDS) resource generator\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/cluster.go` — Cluster building logic\n- `pilot/pkg/features/xds.go` — Feature flags (debounce, push throttle, caching)\n- `pilot/pkg/bootstrap/discovery.go` — Server initialization\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
